Repoint is then **byte-identical**. **New `tests/test_wellness_reader_equality.py`** drives one fixture set through the verbatim old reader + the new materialize+read path and asserts identical `recent_wellness` (+ the `TestRecentWellness`/`TestAssembleBundle` rewrites for the 1-read shape). Suite **3582/30**. `canonical_wellness` `TestCoalesce` now owns the coalesce-semantics tests. Closing `ÔÇŽSlice2_3_2026_06_28ÔÇŽ`. **DEFERRED (decide at build):** the optional `/wellness` chart repoint (`routes/wellness.py`); `coaching.get_wellness_summary` stays out of scope (v1-only). **LIVE-VERIFY still blocked on data** (Andy re-uploads post-#934-deploy Ôćĺ canonical fills Ôćĺ the repointed reader has rows).

## Layer 3 / process ÔÇö Slice 3 gating + collision + CI quirk (2026-06-22)

- **Parallel-build collision (lesson).** #865 (a session branch) and #868 (another session) both built #214/#213 Slice 2; #868 merged first, #865 closed as superseded. The duplicate was invisible until `git fetch origin main` during rebase. **When running concurrent Claude sessions on one epic, at session start `git fetch origin main` + check the issue (e.g. #213/#214) for an existing PR/branch/merged commit before building.** Rule #9 extended to the remote.
- **CI-trigger quirk.** Commits pushed from a Claude session branch (container git path) may **not** trigger the `CI` workflow (`.github/workflows/ci.yml`), even though the commit reaches GitHub and Vercel builds it (Vercel uses its own webhook). Symptom: PR head shows only the `Vercel` status; `actions_list` shows zero CI runs for the branch while other `claude/*` PRs trigger fine. **Workaround:** `actions_run_trigger run_workflow` (`workflow_dispatch`) on `ci.yml` against the branch ÔÇö its jobs post the required check contexts on the head commit by name, satisfying branch protection; auto-merge then fires. (Confirmed 2026-06-22, run #763.)
- **Layer 3D #213 staleness re-fire SHIPPED as #880's Reading-B; #881 Reading-A consolidated out (2026-06-22).** **Parallel-build collision:** #881 (this branch) built the staleness fingerprint as **Reading-A** (`evaluated_against` = *computed* 2A/2C/2D payload hashes, `compute_gate_fingerprint`); #880 (`claude/serene-newton-igye62`, `5959ed7`) shipped the same #213 staleness as **Reading-B** ÔÇö `input_fingerprint` = a SHA-256 over the **raw leaf inputs** (`compute_gate_input_fingerprint`, no LLM) **plus the on-view consumer** (`routes/plan_create.py` re-entry/acknowledge/generate Ôćĺ re-kick the row to `generating` = the async recompute via the poller). Both merged (disjoint lines, never CI'd together) Ôćĺ main briefly carried both, mine dead (unread) + polluting `evaluated_against`. **Andy: consolidate on Reading-B** (cheaper ÔÇö no cone rebuild; already ships the consumer). Cleanup PR reverts #881's Reading-A code + rewrites `Layer3D_Spec` ┬ž6.1/┬ž6.1.1/┬ž11.2 to Reading-B; `evaluated_against` restored to the etl-provenance stamp. Combined main green (128 gate+#880 tests). The earlier **#874** (`stale: bool` + sync re-gate) was closed superseded before all this. **Review-screen UX remainder SHIPPED (2026-06-22, branch `claude/brave-rubin-ikblc4`):** (1) `[Fix this]` revise links (`plan_create._build_revise_urls` Ôćĺ `profile.injuries`=`injuries.list_entries`, `profile.disciplines`/`.nutrition`/`.availability`=**`profile.edit`** [Rule #9: NOT `locales.edit_profile` ÔÇö that's the per-locale *equipment* editor; the three live on the athlete profile page], `h2.*`=**`race_events.edit_race`** [not the handoff's `race_event_edit`]; fail-safe, falls back to the text stub for unmapped `h3.*` / unresolvable surfaces); (2) 3A/3B prompt-rev pointer comments (bump `LAYER3_GATE_PROMPT_REVISION`); (3) `_rekick_stale_gate` Rule #15 telemetry print. The #874 `5b4de06` form/`_REVISE_TARGET_ENDPOINTS` reuse was moot ÔÇö `5b4de06` is gone from the remote (closed branch), and #880's fingerprint auto-detects staleness on re-entry so a plain link suffices (no `revised`-resolution form needed). **Still owed: only live-verify (Andy)** ÔÇö park a plan Ôćĺ each item links to the right editor; edit a field, re-enter `/review` Ôćĺ re-kicks + re-evaluates; `/admin/logs` shows `_rekick_stale_gate:`. Then **3C** (#844) is all that's left on the 3D node. Handoffs `ÔÇŽSlice3a_FingerprintÔÇŽ` (┬ž9 = consolidation) + `ÔÇŽLayer3D_ReviseLinks_213ÔÇŽ` (this slice).
- **Test-run gotcha + fix (container, 2026-06-22).** Route modules (`routes.plan_create`, ÔÇŽ) open a Neon connect **at import time**, which **hangs** in the container (Neon egress blocked) ÔÇö so any test importing the Flask app (e.g. `tests/test_layer3d_wiring.py`) hangs on collection. **Fix (from #880's handoff, verified this session ÔÇö 62 passed incl. the wiring suite):** point `DATABASE_URL` at a dead localhost so the import-time connect *fast-fails* instead of hanging ÔÇö `DATABASE_URL="postgresql://u:p@127.0.0.1:5999/none?connect_timeout=2" /tmp/venv/bin/python -m pytest tests/test_layer3d_wiring.py tests/test_layer3d_gate.py -q` ÔÇö run with `dangerouslyDisableSandbox: true` + a `timeout` (else the harness sandbox terminates any pytest that touches network mid-collection: silent 0-byte output, exit 1). App-free files (e.g. `tests/test_layer3d_gate.py`) run without the shim; front-load a `tests/test_layer4_*.py` to dodge the isolated-single-file circular-import quirk.
- **3C SHIPPED + surfacing story complete (2026-06-23).** The line above ("3C is all that's left on the 3D node") is now closed: 3C built as #844/#911 (CN-1/CN-2 + `surface_orphaned_flags`), then **Item B** (green-plan coaching notes) shipped on `claude/awesome-ride-5j0m3k` (`f6deab7`, PR-pending) ÔÇö informational gate items now list on the plan home (`view_plan` Ôćĺ `view.html` via `_plan_coaching_notes`), closing the gap where a green plan hid its surfaced flags. **Remaining 3C levers (none buildable now, per the kickoff ┬ž2 map `ÔÇŽLayer3C_ConflictDetection_NextStepsÔÇŽ`):** Item A flagÔćĺ`warning` promotions are **prod-signal-gated** (flip a ┬ž7.1 Ôśů into `_FLAG_WARNING` only on a real informational miss); Item C CN-3+ new detectors are **STOP-AND-ASK** (Trigger #5 + spec-first; don't build speculatively). **Owed live-verifies (Andy):** the #213 revise-links/staleness walk (above, still open) + the optional Item-B visual check (a green plan with Ôëą1 informational flag shows the Coaching-notes panel ÔÇö render-test-covered). 3C may be done for v1.

## #803 StrengthExercise resolution-tier crash ÔÇö deterministic fix, all 4 synth paths (2026-06-20; PR [#807](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/807), auto-merge armed) ÔÇö pushed; plan-regen live-verify owed
- **Root cause:** the synthesizer emitted **tier-1 (exact)** `StrengthExercise` picks that *also* carried a `substitute_text` Ôćĺ the `StrengthExercise` tierÔćöfield validator (`payload._check_resolution_tier`) raised Ôćĺ the Build block fumbled (no retry budget on the long block call) Ôćĺ the whole plan failed (pv76/pv77). It's a cross-field rule the JSON tool schema can't express + the prompt only half-stated. **#777 exposed it** (MTB/packraft strength pool 0Ôćĺ37 turned the substitution path ON).
- **Fix (option C ÔÇö deterministic, Andy-ratified):** `per_phase._apply_strength_resolution(raw_sessions, layer2c_payloads)` + `_strength_resolution_fields(rx)` overwrite `resolution_tier`/`substitute_text`/`proxy_origin_id` from each pick's **enum-locked `exercise_id` Ôćĺ 2C resolution at the session's locale**, *before* `StrengthExercise(**e)`. Wired at **all four** construction sites (`per_phase` / `single_session` [locale-gated] / `plan_refresh` / `race_week_brief`). Helpers in `per_phase`; siblings already import it (no new cycle). `per_phase.SYSTEM_PROMPT` strength bullet rewritten (system derives the tier) + `LAYER4_PROMPT_REVISION 18Ôćĺ19`. Strict `model_validator` kept as backstop. No schema/contract/migration change. **3001 passed / 30 skipped.**
- **LIVE-VERIFY owed (Andy-action ÔÇö container can't run plan-gen):** regenerate the MTB+packraft PGE plan Ôćĺ reaches `ready`, no `StrengthExercise` `ValidationError` in `/admin/logs`. **Folds into the Plan-75 regen below** (same arc ÔÇö #777 turned on the path #803 fixes).
- **Carried, separate (NOT fixed ÔÇö Rule #16):** an over-budget attempt-1 that parse-fails gets no retry, so one bad block call still fumbles the plan. #803 removes the *most-likely* parse failure; the no-retry-on-overbudget structural issue is its own follow-up if it recurs.

## #339 cross-discipline variety substitution (2026-06-20; PRs #800 `3f2657e` + #802) ÔÇö SHIPPED + #339 CLOSED; live-verify owed
- **What:** the four Layer-4 synthesizers now MAY render an **easy** cardio session as a training-equivalent discipline **within the same locomotion mode** when (and only when) the athlete's durable Coaching Memory states a variety / cross-training preference. **Foot group** (roadÔćötrailÔćötreadmillÔćöhike) shipped in **#800**; **wheel group** (roadÔćögravelÔćöMTB) in **#802**. `VARIETY_CARVEOUT_PROMPT_SECTION` (per_phase, path-neutral) is in per_phase's `SYSTEM_PROMPT` + appended by plan_refresh / single_session / race_week_brief. **Invariants:** easy-typed only; per-discipline counts + the long (LSD) + every quality session stay on the race discipline; minority of easy volume; **never across modes** (a bike for a run); **self-limiting guard** defers to an explicit single-session sport pick + race-week specificity (so it's inert on those two paths).
- **Coaching Memory render extended:** #690/#797 rendered the durable Coaching Memory block in per_phase only; #339 extends the render to plan_refresh / single_session / race_week_brief (reuses `_format_coaching_memory` + `coaching_preferences` ÔÇö no duplicate plumbing). `LAYER4_PROMPT_REVISION 16Ôćĺ17 (#800) Ôćĺ 18 (#802)`.
- **Reconciliation note:** #339's prerequisite plumbing was being built twice ÔÇö **#797** (merged after this branch was cut) had already landed the Coaching Memory store under `coaching_preferences` / `_format_coaching_memory`; the in-flight branch was reset onto `main` and rebuilt on #797's symbols (duplicate discarded). The #800Ôćĺ#802 split was the foot-only-then-wheel correction (Andy "reopen #339, add bike now"): #800 was foot-only and mislabeled the within-cycling roadÔćöMTB swap as "cross cardio mode"; #802 generalized to within-mode equivalents + corrected the cross-mode meaning to footÔćöwheelÔćöwater.
- **LIVE-VERIFY owed (Andy-action):** regen a plan for an athlete with a stated variety pref in Coaching Memory Ôćĺ an EASY trail-run slot may render as an easy road run (and an easy MTB slot as an easy road-bike spin); the long + quality sessions stay on the race discipline; the swap is named in `coaching_intent`; the cache bump (18) regenerated the plan. Fix: coerce empty `observed_at`ÔćĺNULL + wrap the raw write in a `SAVEPOINT` so a corroboration-write failure is logged (`[provider-raw] ÔÇŽ SKIPPED`) and swallowed, never breaking the athlete's log. **Root-caused by reproducing against a local Postgres** ÔÇö the Slice-2c unit tests used a fake DB, so the live SQL never ran in CI (the coverage gap below).

Dedup keys = FIT content hashes. **Both ┬ž5 live-verify items closed.**

## FIT-import prod incident + hub uploader unify (2026-06-19) ÔÇö FIXED; one residual (#747)
- **`init_postgres` silently aborted on every cold start since #733 (2026-06-18).** A `;` inside a SQL comment in `PG_SCHEMA` broke the char-based `PG_SCHEMA.split(';')` into a bare-text fragment that syntax-errored in the UNGUARDED schema loop (caught only by app.py's broad `except` Ôćĺ "DB init skipped"). Net: **no schema/migration from #733 on reached prod** ÔÇö `provider_value_map`, `provider_raw_record` (Slice 1), `cardio_log.discipline_id` (Slice 2a) all absent until **PR #742** (remove the `;` + per-statement-guard the schema loop + Rule #15 log + `tests/test_init_db_schema.py`). Surfaced as a prod `500 UndefinedColumn discipline_id` on a real FIT import. **Verified fixed via `neon-query`:** provider_value_map (263 rows) + provider_raw_record + discipline_id now live.
- **┬ž5 Slice-2 live-verify (MTB) ÔÇö DONE:** re-import landed `cardio_log` row `Mountain Biking, discipline_id=D-008`. Trail-run Ôćĺ D-001 half still optional (not required).
- **RESIDUAL ÔÇö issue [#747](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/747) (low-pri hardening):** (1) `PG_SCHEMA.split(';')` is char-based ÔÇö any `;` in a string literal / CHECK / comment re-breaks it (the regression test guards comments only; the splitter is the real fragility); (2) the seed steps AFTER the migration loop in `init_postgres` are still unguarded. Acute bug fixed + regression-tested; this is "don't let the class recur structurally."
- **Hub FIT uploader unified (PRs #744 / #746):** the Connections-hub drop card was a fake single-file form Ôćĺ now the real multi-file bulk uploader (`data-bulk-*`), and `import_bulk` routes **both** workout + wellness FITs by FileId kind via a shared `_ingest_wellness_fit` helper. A window-level file-drop guard in `app.js` keeps a stray drop from navigating the browser to the file. The dedicated `/import-wellness` page is untouched.
- **Standing lesson (Rule #9/#10 gap):** a green `verify-handoff.sh` + clean on-disk anchors do **not** prove prod applied a migration. The container can't reach Neon, so for any "schema/migration is live" claim, a read-only `neon-query` is the only proof of the DB half.

Spec only ÔÇö no code.
- **Batch 3 finding (recorded so nobody re-derives it):** TrainingPeaks = a real bidirectional OAuth2 partner API (inbound workouts/zones/`ftp_w`/HRV/weight + outbound `Structure` push) but **partner-access-gated** (no personal use, reportedly paused) ÔÇö capability Ôëá access; its `rowing` WorkoutType is **bucket-3** (training modality, not a discipline ÔÇö ┬ž6 mint reversed); it's a hub-of-hubs (auto-aggregates Oura/WHOOP/Garmin Ôćĺ dedup risk). **Zwift = no inbound API at all** Ôćĺ cardio arrives via Strava/FIT (don't build a Zwift connector); outbound = generate `.zwo`. Both are primarily **Wave-3b outbound**.

- **┬ž6 Rowing mint ÔÇö REVERSED (Andy 2026-06-18). NO D-033, NO follow-up layer0 task.** On-water rowing isn't frequent in our market and won't ever be a race leg (the bar for a canon discipline), so Rowing stays **bucket-3** and erg-rowing is already covered by the existing `Rowing ergometer` machine in the Layer-4 feasibility cascade (`session_feasibility._DISCIPLINE_INDOOR_MACHINES`, paddle disciplines). The earlier "mint Rowing D-033" follow-up is **cancelled** ÔÇö `discipline_canon.py` is untouched. Generalized in the new **doc ┬ž12 (discipline vs. training-modality/equipment)**: stair/erg/treadmill/rollerski are *machines*, walking is coarse `_plan_sport_type`, yoga/HIIT/CrossFit are mobility/strength categories ÔÇö none are disciplines; same no-padding instinct as #692 (fold indoor bikes into `Cycling trainer`). The one real build-wave gap: **carry an inbound indoor/machine flag** (Strava `VirtualRide`/`StairStepper`, RWGPS `is_stationary`, Wahoo `workout_type_location_id`) in `raw_payload`.

The #884 gear/craft model v3 (Decision 10) **promotes rollerskis to owned dryland *gear*** ÔÇö a degraded D-028 substitute ranked above the gym ski-erg (`gear_discipline_aliases` rank 2, migration `0023`). The matrix's *inbound-classification* call is unchanged (a `RollerSki` activity still maps to D-028, raw-flagged); only the ownership/feasibility treatment is added. Add a one-line ┬ž12 footnote so the docs don't drift.
- **Multi-source precedence ÔÇö RATIFIED (Andy 2026-06-18): freshest-timestamp-wins**, de-dup hub-of-hubs (TP) re-emits by source-of-origin. (Applies to `sleep_score`/`resting_hr_bpm`/`body_mass_kg`/`ftp_w`/`hrv_rmssd_ms`, each from 2ÔÇô3 providers.)

## Ops automation / operating model ÔÇö LIVE (2026-06-15; record issue #630)

**This changed how we work. Read it before doing prod DB ops or merges.** The web container can't reach Neon, but GitHub Actions can ÔÇö so prod DB work + merges run in the cloud, Claude drives them, and Andy only approves the irreversible bits ("decide-not-do"; Andy is mobile / device-changing, consistent access = Claude Code web/Android). All of the below is built, merged, and **test-fired green** this session.

**Operating flow (default for every change):** Claude opens a PR Ôćĺ `enable_pr_auto_merge` (**MERGE** ÔÇö real merge commit, Andy 2026-06-29; not squash) Ôćĺ it **self-merges once required checks pass**. Branch protection on `main`: required checks (`Python unit suite (stubbed)` / `JS harness (jsdom)` / `Layer 0 integrity gate`), **0 approvals** (solo can't self-approve ÔÇö do NOT require reviews or it deadlocks), **admin-bypass off**. Auto-merge is enabled repo-wide. Don't merge mid-run; let it land. `.github/CODEOWNERS` auto-requests Andy's review on `etl/migrations/` (soft nudge only ÔÇö never flip on "require code-owner review").

> **GOTCHA ÔÇö MCP-opened PRs don't trigger `ci.yml` (found 2026-06-29, #884 PR-3).** A PR opened via the GitHub MCP `create_pull_request` tool does **not** fire the `on: pull_request` workflow (GitHub suppresses workflow runs from that token to prevent recursion), so the three required checks never register and the PR can't satisfy branch protection ÔÇö it strands with "Expected ÔÇö waiting for status." (This stranded #990.) **Fix:** after opening such a PR, trigger CI explicitly ÔÇö `actions_run_trigger run_workflow` on **`ci.yml` with `ref=<branch>`**. All three required jobs run under `workflow_dispatch` (`if: github.event_name != 'schedule'`), attach as check runs on the PR head SHA, and release auto-merge. (Pushing to the feature branch does NOT help ÔÇö `ci.yml`'s `push` trigger is `branches:[main]` only.)

**Triggerable workflows** (Claude via `actions_run_trigger run_workflow`, or Andy via Actions tab Ôćĺ Run workflow):
- **`layer0-apply.yml`** ÔÇö applies `etl/migrations/layer0/*.sql` to prod Neon, **gated by the `production` GitHub Environment** (required reviewer = Andy Ôćĺ one tap to approve; admin-bypass off; prevent-self-review off so Andy can approve Claude-triggered runs). Idempotent Ôćĺ safe to re-run. **This replaces the old "Andy pastes SQL into the Neon editor" step.**
- **`layer0-redump.yml`** (input `version`, default next) ÔÇö `pg_dump`s live `layer0` Ôćĺ `etl/output/layer0_etl_v<ver>.sql` on branch `claude/layer0-baseline-v<ver>`; then open the PR so the `layer0-gate` validates the snapshot before merge. Keeps the committed baseline in lockstep with live (prevents the drift that caused #616).
- **`neon-query.yml`** (input `query`) ÔÇö read-only diagnostic SELECT vs prod via the read-only role; read-only enforced by role grants + `default_transaction_read_only=on`; result in the job log (Claude reads via `get_job_logs`).
- **`layer0-validate-live.yml`** ÔÇö **nightly** (cron `0 7 * * *`) + manual `validate_layer0` vs **live** prod via the read-only role; catches live integrity drift (the #616 `primary_movement`-clobber class) automatically + emails Andy on failure. First run PASS.

**Secrets / gates (one-time, all set):** `NEON_DATABASE_URL` (write ÔÇö apply/redump) ┬Ě `NEON_RO_DATABASE_URL` (read-only Neon role `claude_ro`, SELECT on `layer0`+`public` ÔÇö diag/validate-live) ┬Ě `production` environment (required reviewer = @ahorn885).

**Prod logs (Rule #14 ÔÇö no more traceback-pasting):** `GET /admin/logs?token=<DIAG_TOKEN>` (optional `&q=<substr>&minutes=N`), fetched via the **Vercel MCP `mcp__Vercel__web_fetch_vercel_url`** tool ÔÇö **NOT plain `WebFetch`**. The prod deployment is behind Vercel Authentication: an anonymous fetcher (`WebFetch`) 403s at the Vercel edge *before* the app's token gate, so a 403 there is an auth-layer block, not a bad token. The Vercel MCP tool carries the team's Vercel auth Ôćĺ 200 (confirmed 2026-06-16; `get_access_to_vercel_url` is the fallback for cookie-based share links). Andy pastes the current `DIAG_TOKEN` per debugging session (**chat-only, never commit**); rotated 2026-06-16 (`sk_ÔÇŽ` form, supersedes `0dKHoR2ÔÇŽ`). Preferred over the truncating Vercel runtime-log MCP.

**Local sync:** `.claude/settings.json` has a `SessionStart` `git pull --ff-only` hook so Andy's local clone auto-syncs with web-session merges.

## T3 plan-refresh fixes (2026-06-13, PR #569 + #572) ÔÇö DONE; one live re-verify owed (post-#572)

**PR [#569](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/569) (`Closes #570`, branch `claude/plan-65-refresh-r8tclv`) squash-merged to `main`.** The live T3-refresh verify owed by the #566/#208 handoff surfaced that **T3 refresh had never worked**: `routes/plan_refresh.py` never passed `plan_start_date` to `orchestrate_plan_refresh`, so every T3 (cross-phase) refresh failed `_validate_inputs` with `plan_start_date_missing` (T1/T2 don't require it Ôćĺ silent). Fix: `_resolve_plan_start_date` walks `refresh_parent_version_id` to the root `plan_create` row's `scope_start_date` (the plan's true start, NOT the refresh window), threaded through `build_refresh_advance_ctx` Ôćĺ `run_refresh_orchestration`. **Code-only, NO DDL, nothing to deploy.** Handoff: `V5_Implementation_T3RefreshPlanStartDateFix_2026_06_13_Closing_Handoff_v1.md`.

- Ôťů **#208 async/resumable refresh ÔÇö confirmed live-correct.** The watch proved the plumbing: POSTÔćĺ302ÔćĺprogressÔćĺcron/poller passes, cron solo-drove after tab-close, advance-lock guard held, graceful `_mark_plan_failed` (no 504). The owed "live refresh verify" from #566 is effectively discharged for the async machinery.
- Ôťů **#569 `plan_start_date` fix ÔÇö CONFIRMED LIVE (2026-06-13).** The owed re-verify ran (T3 refresh of pv=65 Ôćĺ pv=67, `created_via=plan_refresh_t3`); pv=67 **cleared `_validate_inputs`** ÔÇö no `plan_start_date_missing`. T3 refresh now reaches real synthesis.

Create's per-phase block-mode now calls the same helper (behavior-preserving ÔÇö its blocks are ÔëĄ21,600). +4 tests; full suite 2366; CI green. **Code-only, NO DDL.** Handoff: `V5_Implementation_T3RefreshOutputBudgetTruncationFix_2026_06_13_Closing_Handoff_v1.md`.

## Locations privacy surfacing (2026-06-11, PR #535) ÔÇö DONE, NO migration owed

**PR [#535](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/535) squash-merged to `main`, branch `claude/github-issue-446-lhnk9c`.** Closes **#446** (Track 1 child of #434; Locations epic #427). New locations derived privacy purely from category with no visible indicator and no override ÔÇö so a residence Mapbox geocoded as `commercial_gym` silently landed shareable ("everything defaults to shared, there's no toggle").

- **UI surfacing, not a model change** (per the issue spec note). `gym_profiles.private` stays source-of-truth; the previously-**dormant** `locale_profiles.sharing_opt_out` column (declared but never read/written) now carries the explicit choice from locale-creation Ôćĺ profile-build. Effective `private = (category Ôłł RESIDENTIAL_CATEGORIES) OR sharing_opt_out` via `_resolve_private` / `_category_default_private` in `routes/locales.py`. The opt-out can only **tighten** ÔÇö residences are never crowd-shareable (the safe default).
- Live private/shared **chip** + **opt-out toggle**: manual `new.html` form (chip updates as category is picked; nonce'd inline JS per the terrain-editor precedent), each Mapbox result card, and the edit `form.html` (own/build mode; residences show a locked "Private" state; `shared_inherit` mode untouched ÔÇö the shared profile's privacy is its creator's).
- **Crowd-source filtering now reads the explicit flag:** `_find_gym_profile` excludes `private` rows (a peer at the same `mapbox_id` builds their own profile instead of inheriting one its creator marked private; the creator still reaches their own via the `gym_profile_id` link). `delete_locale` cleanup is flag-driven (`created_by_user_id = uid AND COALESCE(private,FALSE)=TRUE`), not re-derived from category ÔÇö prevents orphaned private profiles from opted-out shareable locales.
- Tests: `tests/test_locales.py` (+10 ÔÇö `_resolve_private`/`_category_default_private` truth table, `_find_gym_profile` exclusion, build-path opt-out Ôćĺ `private`, flag-driven delete) + render smoke `tests/test_redesign_locales_form_render.py` updated for the new template contract. CI green (Vercel + stubbed unit suite).
- Ôťů **NO Neon migration owed** ÔÇö both `gym_profiles.private` and `locale_profiles.sharing_opt_out` already exist on prod (landed with the Track 1 DDL, item 0 below). Pure code/UI change; live the moment the deploy lands.

   real ids, never invent; per-phase dose 2/2/1/1; RM/RPE). **`movement_patterns` threaded**
   through 2C (`layer0.exercises.movement_patterns` Ôćĺ query Ôćĺ `ResolvedExercise`) Ôćĺ pattern
   ranking + **data-driven core/accessory** (core = Critical/High priority + compound pattern).
   **Slice 2:** `strength_frequency_band` advisory validator (`warning`-only). **NO migration.**
   First post-merge cold plan re-synthesizes cold (prompt + 2C cache-key shift ÔÇö expected).

     2/2/1/1 ships; personalizing it by the athlete's 3A strength state is not wired ÔÇö needs the
     3A strength-state field). **Phase 2b (#335):** `rx_engine` absolute loads from logged
     capacity (bootstrap `strength_benchmarks`). **Phase 3 (#298/#341):** multi-locale cluster.
8. **pv=57 carry-forward (non-blocking; from the pulled diag logs, 2026-06-05).**
   - **ÔÜá CORRECTION to item 6.1's "real ~300s gateway":** that is **WRONG**. The kill is the
     **800s `FUNCTION_INVOCATION_TIMEOUT`** (request `bd6z7-ÔÇŽ`, `Duration: 800047ms`), not a
     300s gateway. The cone is a **clean HIT** on reclaim (`ibundle` stable), not re-computing.
     The pv=57 stall was the #335 strength thrash (item 7), not latency/gateway.
   - **`PLAN_GEN_FUNCTION_CAP_S` env tune (Andy's call, optional, reversible):** currently **300**
     (budget 30s Ôćĺ 1 block/pass, clean). With #335 removing the thrash and the real ceiling
     confirmed at **800s**, raising back toward **800** (budget ~470s Ôćĺ ~2 blocks/pass) is faster
     and safe. The earlier "don't raise it" caution was under the now-disproven 300s-gateway
     hypothesis. **Not required** for a successful run.
   - **Layer 2B cache-key drift:** at 12:35 only `l2b` drifted (`f17c69d0`Ôćĺ`5fcf7380`) while every
     other cone hash held Ôćĺ re-keys all blocks Ôćĺ re-synth churn. The #199/#294 determinism class,
     now on Layer 2B. Worth a determinism fix (day-anchor / pin the drifting field).
   - **Advance-lock TTL (310s) < real max function duration (800s):** a long pass outlives its
     own lock Ôćĺ a concurrent pass can reclaim mid-flight (duplicate Anthropic spend on a stuck
     block). Align the TTL to the real ceiling, or cap pass wall-clock < TTL.
9. **pv=58 carry-forward ÔÇö the per-week volume periodization grid SHIPPED + #316 CLOSED (2026-06-05, PR #422 merged).**
   Andy raised `PLAN_GEN_FUNCTION_CAP_S` to **800** (the item-8 env tune ÔÇö now done) and re-ran a cold
   plan (pv=58); it stalled at `Build:w2`. Untruncated logs root-caused **two engines**: **(A)** the
   synthesizer's first attempt (`extended_thinking_budget=5000` + `tool_choice:auto`) ran away to
   `max_tokens` (418s, empty) before the forced retry did the real work in 110s ÔÇö each failed attempt
   Ôëł530s, ungated; **(B)** `volume_band` graded each week against a flat per-phase band Ôćĺ `Build:w2`

   band per week + drops the PR #315 demotion; prompt feeds concrete per-week targets; `recovery_week`

   - **ÔÜá Engine A is UNFIXED ÔÇö #423 (the next lever).** The 418s thinking-first runaway + ungated first
     attempt is the latency engine; Andy deferred it ("no time-limit work until the data problem is
     sorted"). Drop `extended_thinking_budget`Ôćĺ0 for block synthesis (forced retry already does the work
     in ~110s) and gate/headroom the first attempt. **A dense week can still 504 even though validation
     now passes** ÔÇö that's #423, not the grid.
   - **Grid v2 = #424 (committed):** 3A coupling ÔÇö modulate ramp steepness by `recent_trajectory` /

- 1 **D-77 poller 500 regression ÔÇö `'generating'`-mapping + client give-up cap fix (2026-05-29, PR #312).** PR #311 added two `{"status": "generating", ...}` returns to `_advance_plan_generation` (concurrency guard Ôćĺ `advance_in_progress_elsewhere`; per-invocation budget Ôćĺ `budget_partial_progress`) but the poller route `generate_plan` was never taught to handle them ÔÇö it fell through to `jsonify({"status": "failed", "error": outcome['error']})`, KeyError-ing on the missing key Ôćĺ **HTTP 500 on every intermediate poll**. The budget makes `budget_partial_progress` the *normal* path for any plan needing >1 pass, so essentially every real multi-block plan 500'd to the client's give-up copy ("This is taking longer than expected. Please try again.") even though the cone was healthy and caching blocks. Fix: (1) `generate_plan` maps `'generating'` Ôćĺ `{"status":"generating"}` (keep-polling); (2) `templates/plan_create/progress.html` swaps the *total*-poll cap (`MAX_ATTEMPTS=20` ÔÇö far too few now each pass caches ~1 week-block) for a *consecutive-transport-failure* cap (a clean response resets it); the server-side `_STALL_WALLCLOCK_S=900`s backstop stays the real terminal guard. 2 code/template files + `tests/test_routes_plan_create.py` (+5 `TestGeneratePlanRoute`); 50 passed in-file, 160 combined. No migration. **This is a prerequisite for owed-deploy #1 (the convergence re-run) ÔÇö see that entry.** (Walk, deployed + `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`: 1: create a fresh PGE 2026 plan; the progress screen runs for many minutes past the old ~20-poll wall, elapsed counter climbing, and opens the plan on `ready` ÔÇö no premature "taking longer than expected". 2: mid-flight, `POST /plans/v2/<id>/generate` returns `200 {"status":"generating"}` in devtoolsÔćĺNetwork, not 500. 3: a genuinely stuck unit still fails loudly via the 900s server backstop Ôćĺ the poller shows the stored failure message, not the generic give-up copy.)

- Ôťů **Plan-gen non-convergence ÔÇö ROOT CAUSE FIXED 2026-05-27 (branch `claude/plan-gen-timeout-logs-caH8Q`).** The instrumented re-run (`plan_version_id=27`) pinned the stall to TWO independent bugs, both now fixed. **(1) Non-deterministic cache keys (the primary bug):** `Layer1Payload.as_of` + `Layer2APayload.rationale_metadata.generated_at` carried a full-precision `datetime.utcnow()` hashed into `layer1_hash`/`layer2a_hash`, which fold into EVERY Layer 4 cache key ÔÇö so 3A + 3B re-ran cold on every resumable pass (live-run `Layer3A/3BEvidenceBasisWarning` in 17/17 prod passes, ~150s/pass) and any synthesized block was orphaned next pass Ôćĺ D-77 monotonic convergence was structurally impossible (this is why decomposition never helped, and it **overturns the "warm 3A/3B cone" claim in the superseded note below** ÔÇö the cone NEVER cached across passes; the predecessor had no per-layer cache instrumentation). Fixed by day-anchoring both timestamps (neither is consumed ÔÇö pure provenance; matches the 3A `as_of` day-granular semantics). **(2) Synthesizer output starvation:** `attempt 1/3 llm call 142528ms (out=9000)` then `tool_args keys=[]` ÔÇö under thinking the ceiling is `max_tokens(4000)+budget(5000)=9000`, the model spent it all thinking and emitted a contentless tool call Ôćĺ no block cached. Fixed in `invoke_tool_call`: an empty tool call now fires the existing forced-tool retry (thinking off Ôćĺ full output budget, can't decline). Plus a structural **per-block budget** (`_PER_BLOCK_BUDGET_MS=120_000`) in `synthesize_phase`: best-effort accept (caches Ôćĺ progress) or fast terminal (`synthesis_budget_exhausted`), never 504-loops. 4 code files + 13 tests; `Layer4_Spec ┬ž11.5` updated. The two failed `plan_version_id=29` runs 504-looped with `max_tokens=9200` live + `schema_violation` GONE but `accepted=True` never firing ÔÇö i.e. NO block ever converged. **Bug A (the convergence root cause, PR #199):** a SECOND instance of the c4f9160 cache-key non-determinism bug, which that fix missed ÔÇö `Layer2EPayload.computed_at` (`layer2e/builder.py:1156`) was stamped full-microsecond `datetime.now()`; the cone rebuilds every resumable pass and `computed_at` folds into `layer2e_hash` Ôćĺ `plan_create_key` Ôćĺ EVERY `compute_block_cache_key`, so each pass minted different block keys Ôćĺ every synthesized block orphaned Ôćĺ re-synthesized from scratch each pass Ôćĺ 504-loop re-burning the full extended-thinking synthesis each minute (the ~$50). 2E runs AFTER 3B, so it poisons Layer 4 keys but not 3A/3B ÔÇö which is why 3A/3B cached fine and only Layer 4 looped, and why the earlier "warm 3A/3B" reads were consistent with a still-broken Layer 4. It also silently defeated the stall backstop (orphan rows kept `_count_cached_blocks` climbing Ôćĺ never plateaued Ôćĺ never tripped). Fix: day-anchor `computed_at` to the cone's logical `today`. Diagnostics added so the next incident is one-read: `cached_wrappers.py` logs `call_cache_key` + each component layer-hash per pass (drift names the guilty layer); `cache.py` logs per-block cache HIT/MISS. **Bug B (PR #200):** after PR #199 deployed, new plans `pv=30..33` failed IMMEDIATELY (`_advance_plan_generation: D-77 stall backstop tripped` on the first pass ÔÇö impossible for a 900s gate on a brand-new plan). Cause: `_generation_stalled` measured `NOW() - MAX(block.created_at)` scoped to the USER, and `pv=29`'s orphaned rows (>1h old) anchored the window in the past Ôćĺ false-trip on every new plan (bites any user with a prior failed plan). Fix: bound `_generation_stalled` + `_count_cached_blocks` to `created_at >= pv.created_at` (this plan's own progress only). subsequent `python -m etl.layer0.run` invocations on May 10 + May 20 re-introduced workbook-shape legacy rows at v1.3.1 + v2.4-prep and superseded the structured ones). SET superseded_at = NOW() WHERE terrain_id IS NULL AND superseded_at IS NULL`. **Warning carried forward**: do NOT run `python -m etl.layer0.run` against production Neon until the ETL drift fix (Bucket C sub-item (k)) lands ÔÇö the run will undo the manual data fix.
